Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 178, the final release of the Apollo 14 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Zerlina 56, Luminary 210, and Luminary 131, previously transcribed from digitized copies of those programs. The code was created by combining the three, using Zerlina 56 as a base, since it was based off of Luminary 183. The differences between the three were carefully merged using the Luminary memos as a guide, with all changes made after Luminary 178 being backed out. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152N. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those for the baseline log section mentioned in each file's changelog; the page numbers for a real Luminary 178 listing would be different.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

021758,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021759,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021760,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 178.
021761,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the final
021762,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the flight software for the Lunar Module's
021763,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 14. The
021764,000008:                                                                                                  ##              code has been recreated from copies of Zerlina 56, Luminary
021765,000009:                                                                                                  ##              210, and Luminary 131, as well as many Luminary memos.
021766,000010:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
021767,000011:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 178 in NASA
021768,000012:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021152N, which gives relatively high confidence
021769,000013:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
021770,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 500-611
021771,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
021772,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021773,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021774,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-14 MAS  Created from Zerlina 56.
021775,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2019-09-06 MAS  Removed Zerlina-specific changes, including
021776,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              the call to CDU*SMNB, removal of R12FLAG
021777,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              handling, and changes to downlink numbers.
021778,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Also removed stuff added after Luminary 178,
021779,000023:                                                                                                  ##                              including the branch to NOTSHIFT and handling
021780,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              of AGSCODE.

021783,000027:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021784,000028:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021785,000029:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021786,000030:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021787,000031:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021788,000032: 
021789,000033:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021790,000034:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021791,000035:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021792,000036:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021793,000037:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021794,000038: 
021795,000039:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021796,000040:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021797,000041:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
021798,000042:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
021799,000043:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
021800,000044:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
021801,000045:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021802,000046:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021803,000047:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
021804,000048:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
021805,000049:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
021806,000050:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021807,000051:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021808,000052:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021809,000053:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021810,000054:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021811,000055:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021812,000056:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021813,000057:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021814,000058:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021815,000059:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021816,000060:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
021817,000061:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021818,000062:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
021819,000063: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021820,000064: 
021821,000065: 33,2113                                           BANK     33                                    
021822,000066: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021823,000067: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021824,000068: 
021825,000069: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021826,000070: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

022308,000552:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022309,000553:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022310,000554:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022311,000555:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022312,000556:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022313,000557: 
022314,000558:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022315,000559:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022316,000560:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022317,000561:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022318,000562:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022319,000563:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022320,000564:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022321,000565:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022322,000566:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022323,000567:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022324,000568:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022325,000569:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022326,000570:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022327,000571:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022328,000572:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022329,000573:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022330,000574:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022331,000575:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022332,000576:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022333,000577:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022334,000578:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022335,000579:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022336,000580: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022337,000581: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022338,000582: 24,2462           05340        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022339,000583: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022340,000584: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022341,000585: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022342,000586: 
022343,000587: 24,2466           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022344,000588: 24,2467           11241                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022345,000589: 24,2470           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022346,000590: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022347,000591: 24,2472           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022348,000592: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022349,000593: 24,2474           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022350,000594: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG                              
022351,000595: 24,2476           05364        P25LEM1            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022352,000596: 24,2477           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022353,000597: 24,2500           34743                           CAF      P25FLBIT                              
022354,000598: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022355,000599: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022356,000600: 24,2503           15155                           BZF      ENDOFJOB                              
022357,000601: 24,2504           34747                           CAF      TRACKBIT                              #  IS TRACKFLAG SET?

Page 512 

022359,000603: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022360,000604: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022361,000605: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022362,000606: 24,2510           34757                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022363,000607: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR                               
022364,000608: 24,2512           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE
022365,000609: 24,2513           46123                           CADR     R65LEM                                
022366,000610: 24,2514           02476                           TC       P25LEM1                               #  THEN GO CHECK FLAGS
022367,000611: 24,2515           32526        P25LMWT1           CAF      60SCNDS

022369,000613: 24,2517           02521                           ADRES    P25LEM2

022380,000624:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022381,000625:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022382,000626:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022383,000627:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022384,000628:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022385,000629: 
022386,000630:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022387,000631:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022388,000632:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022389,000633:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022390,000634:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM

022393,000637:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL

022395,000639:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022396,000640:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022397,000641:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022398,000642:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.

022584,000828:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)

022589,000833: 
022590,000834:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022591,000835:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022592,000836:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022593,000837:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL

022604,000848:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022605,000849:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF

022607,000851:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT

022790,001034:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022791,001035:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022792,001036:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022793,001037:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022794,001038:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022795,001039: 
022796,001040:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022797,001041:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022798,001042:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
022799,001043:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022800,001044:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
022801,001045:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022802,001046:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022803,001047:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022804,001048:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
022805,001049:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
022806,001050:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022807,001051:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022808,001052:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022809,001053:                                                                                                  #    N.A.
022810,001054:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED-
022811,001055:                                                                                                  #    ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022812,001056: 24,3221     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022813,001057: 24,3221                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022814,001058: 24,3221           05515        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022815,001059: 24,3222           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022816,001060: 24,3223           00004                           INHINT                                         
022817,001061: 24,3224           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022818,001062: 24,3225           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022819,001063: 24,3226           00003                           RELINT                                         
022820,001064: 24,3227           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022821,001065: 24,3230           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022822,001066: 24,3231           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
022823,001067: 24,3232           33271                           CAF      OCT205                                
022824,001068: 24,3233           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022825,001069: 24,3234           20624                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
022826,001070: 24,3235           03262                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE
022827,001071: 24,3236           03240                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE
022828,001072: 24,3237           03265                           TC       R23LEM3                               #  ENTER- DO ANOTHER MANUVER
022829,001073: 24,3240           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT                                         
022830,001074: 24,3241           04523                           TC       RRLIMCHK                              #  YES - CHECK IF ANTENNA IS WITHIN LIMITS
022831,001075: 24,3242           00035                           ADRES    CDUT                                  
022832,001076: 24,3243           03252                           TC       OUTOFLIM                              #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022833,001077: 24,3244           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  RESTORE DEADBAND TO
022834,001078: 24,3245           40115                           CADR     RESTORDB                              #  ASTRONAUT SELECTED VALUE
022835,001079: 24,3246           00003                           RELINT                                         
022836,001080: 24,3247           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  CLEAR NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022837,001081: 24,3250           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022838,001082: 24,3251           02241                           TC       P20LEMB1                              #  RADAR IS LOCKED ON CONTINUE IN P20

022841,001085: 24,3253           33270                           CAF      OCT501PV

022843,001087: 24,3255           21563                           CADR     PRIOLARM                              #  LIMITS

022860,001104:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022861,001105:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022862,001106:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022863,001107:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022864,001108:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022865,001109: 
022866,001110:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022867,001111:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022868,001112:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022869,001113:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022870,001114:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
022871,001115:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
022872,001116:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
022873,001117:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
022874,001118:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022875,001119:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
022876,001120:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
022877,001121:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
022878,001122:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022879,001123:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
022880,001124:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022881,001125:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022882,001126:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022883,001127:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022884,001128:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022885,001129:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022886,001130:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022887,001131:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022888,001132:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022889,001133:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
022890,001134: 24,3272  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022891,001135: 24,3272                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022892,001136: 24,3272           05515        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022893,001137: 24,3273           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022894,001138: 24,3274           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022895,001139: 24,3275           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022896,001140: 24,3276           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022897,001141: 24,3277           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022898,001142: 24,3300           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022899,001143: 24,3301           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022900,001144: 24,3302           05364        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022901,001145: 24,3303           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022902,001146: 24,3304           33337                           CAF      V16N80                                
022903,001147: 24,3305           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022904,001148: 24,3306           20505                           CADR     PRIODSPR                              
022905,001149: 24,3307           06025                           TC       GOTOV56                               
022906,001150: 24,3310           03314                           TC       R24END                                #  PROCEED EXIT R24 TO P20LEM1
022907,001151: 
022908,001152: 
022909,001153: 24,3311           03320                           TC       R24LEM3                               #  RECYCLE - CALL R61 TO MANEUVER S/C

022954,001198:                                                                                                  #  RRDESSM  WILL RETURN TO CALLER

023170,001414:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023171,001415: 
023172,001416:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023173,001417:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023174,001418:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023175,001419:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023176,001420:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023177,001421:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023178,001422:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023179,001423:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023180,001424:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023181,001425:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023182,001426:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023183,001427:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023184,001428:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023185,001429:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023186,001430:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023187,001431: 
023188,001432:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023189,001433:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023190,001434:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S   (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023191,001435: 
023192,001436:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023193,001437:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023194,001438:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023195,001439:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023196,001440: 
023197,001441:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023198,001442: 
023199,001443:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023200,001444: 
023201,001445:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023202,001446:

023204,001448:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

023249,001493:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023250,001494: 
023251,001495:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023252,001496:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023253,001497:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023254,001498:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023255,001499:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023256,001500:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023257,001501:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023258,001502:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023259,001503:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023260,001504:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023261,001505:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023262,001506:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023263,001507:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023264,001508:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023265,001509:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023266,001510:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023267,001511:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023268,001512:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023269,001513:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023270,001514:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023271,001515: 
023272,001516:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023273,001517:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF

023319,001563:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023320,001564: 
023321,001565:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023322,001566: 
023323,001567:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023324,001568:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023325,001569:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023326,001570:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023327,001571:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023328,001572:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023329,001573:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023330,001574:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023331,001575:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023332,001576:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023333,001577:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023334,001578:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023335,001579: 
023336,001580:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023337,001581:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023338,001582:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023339,001583: 
023340,001584:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023341,001585:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023342,001586: 
023343,001587:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023344,001588: 
023345,001589:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023346,001590:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023347,001591: 
023348,001592:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023349,001593: 
023350,001594:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023351,001595: 
023352,001596: 24,3340                                           BANK     24                                    
023353,001597: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023354,001598: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023355,001599: 
023356,001600: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023357,001601: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023358,001602: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023359,001603: 25,2054           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023360,001604: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
023361,001605: 25,2056           44753                           CS       TURNONBT                              
023362,001606: 25,2057           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

023367,001611:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023368,001612: 
023369,001613:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023370,001614:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023371,001615:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023372,001616:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023373,001617:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023374,001618:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023375,001619:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023376,001620:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023377,001621:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023378,001622:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023379,001623:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023380,001624:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023381,001625:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023382,001626:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023383,001627:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023384,001628:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023385,001629: 
023386,001630:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023387,001631:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023388,001632:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023389,001633: 
023390,001634:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023391,001635: 
023392,001636:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023393,001637:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023394,001638: 
023395,001639:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023396,001640: 
023397,001641:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023398,001642: 
023399,001643: 25,2062           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023400,001644: 25,2063           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023401,001645: 25,2064           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023402,001646: 25,2065           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023403,001647: 25,2066           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023404,001648: 25,2067           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023405,001649: 25,2070           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023406,001650:

023409,001653: 25,2073           54036                           TS       CDUS

023440,001684:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023441,001685:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023442,001686:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023443,001687:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023444,001688:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023445,001689:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023446,001690:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023447,001691:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023448,001692:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023449,001693:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023450,001694:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023451,001695:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023452,001696:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023453,001697:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023454,001698:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023455,001699:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023456,001700:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023457,001701:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023458,001702:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
023459,001703:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023460,001704:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023461,001705:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023462,001706:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023463,001707:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023464,001708: 
023465,001709:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023466,001710:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023467,001711:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023468,001712: 
023469,001713:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023470,001714:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023471,001715: 
023472,001716:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023473,001717:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023474,001718: 
023475,001719:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023476,001720:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023477,001721: 
023478,001722:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
023479,001723: 
023480,001724:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
023481,001725: 
023482,001726: 25,2120           02147        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
023483,001727: 
023484,001728:                                                                                                  #  ALARM 501 DELETED IN DANCE 279 PER PCR 97.
023485,001729:

023487,001731: 25,2122           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023488,001732:

023527,001771:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023528,001772: 
023529,001773:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023530,001774:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023531,001775:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023532,001776:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023533,001777:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023534,001778:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023535,001779:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023536,001780:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023537,001781:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023538,001782:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023539,001783:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023540,001784:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023541,001785:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023542,001786:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023543,001787:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023544,001788:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023545,001789:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023546,001790:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023547,001791:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023548,001792:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023549,001793: 
023550,001794:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023551,001795:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023552,001796:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023553,001797:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023554,001798:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023555,001799: 
023556,001800:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023557,001801:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023558,001802: 
023559,001803:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023560,001804:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023561,001805: 
023562,001806:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023563,001807:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023564,001808: 
023565,001809:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023566,001810: 
023567,001811:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  STDESIG
023568,001812: 
023569,001813: 25,2162           34740        REMODE             CAF      ANTENBIT                              #  DRIVE TRUNNION TO 0 (180)
023570,001814: 25,2163           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  (ERROR COUNTER ALREADY ENABLED)

023620,001864:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023621,001865: 
023622,001866:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023623,001867:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023624,001868:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023625,001869:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023626,001870:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023627,001871:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023628,001872:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023629,001873:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023630,001874:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023631,001875:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023632,001876:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
023633,001877:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023634,001878:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023635,001879:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023636,001880:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
023637,001881: 
023638,001882:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023639,001883:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
023640,001884:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
023641,001885:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023642,001886:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023643,001887: 
023644,001888:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023645,001889:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023646,001890: 
023647,001891:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023648,001892:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023649,001893: 
023650,001894:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023651,001895:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023652,001896: 
023653,001897:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023654,001898: 
023655,001899:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023656,001900:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)
023657,001901:                                                                                                  #  L+1  (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

023708,001952:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023709,001953: 
023710,001954:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023711,001955:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023712,001956:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023713,001957:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023714,001958:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023715,001959:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023716,001960:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023717,001961:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
023718,001962:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023719,001963:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023720,001964:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023721,001965:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023722,001966:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023723,001967:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023724,001968: 
023725,001969:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023726,001970:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023727,001971:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023728,001972: 
023729,001973:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023730,001974:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023731,001975:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
