023814,002058:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023815,002059: 
023816,002060:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023817,002061:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023818,002062:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023819,002063:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023820,002064:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023821,002065:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023822,002066:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023823,002067:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023824,002068:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023825,002069:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023826,002070:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023827,002071:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023828,002072:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023829,002073:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023830,002074:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023831,002075:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023832,002076:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023833,002077:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023834,002078:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023835,002079:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023836,002080:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023837,002081:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023838,002082:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023839,002083: 
023840,002084:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023841,002085:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023842,002086:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
023843,002087:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023844,002088:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023845,002089: 
023846,002090:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023847,002091:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
023848,002092: 
023849,002093:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023850,002094:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023851,002095:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
023852,002096: 
023853,002097:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023854,002098:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023855,002099: 
023856,002100:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023857,002101: 
023858,002102:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023859,002103:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023860,002104:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023900,002144:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023901,002145: 
023902,002146:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023903,002147:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023904,002148:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023905,002149:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023906,002150:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023907,002151:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023908,002152:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023909,002153:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023910,002154:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023911,002155:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
023912,002156:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023913,002157:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
023914,002158:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023915,002159:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023916,002160:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023917,002161:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023918,002162:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023919,002163:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023920,002164:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023921,002165:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023922,002166:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023923,002167: 
023924,002168:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023925,002169:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023926,002170: 
023927,002171:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023928,002172:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023929,002173:

023934,002178:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES

024072,002316:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024073,002317: 
024074,002318:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024075,002319:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024076,002320:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024077,002321:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024078,002322:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024079,002323:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024080,002324:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024081,002325:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024082,002326:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024083,002327:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024084,002328:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024085,002329:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024086,002330:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024087,002331:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024088,002332:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024089,002333:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024090,002334:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024091,002335:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024092,002336:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024093,002337:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024094,002338:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024095,002339:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024096,002340:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024097,002341:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024098,002342:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024099,002343:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024100,002344: 
024101,002345:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024102,002346:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024103,002347:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024104,002348:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024105,002349: 
024106,002350:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024107,002351:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024108,002352: 
024109,002353:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024110,002354:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024111,002355: 
024112,002356:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024113,002357: 
024114,002358:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024115,002359:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024116,002360: 
024117,002361:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024118,002362:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024119,002363:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024120,002364: 
024121,002365: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024167,002411:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024168,002412: 
024169,002413:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024170,002414:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024171,002415:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024172,002416:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024173,002417:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024174,002418:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024175,002419:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024176,002420:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024177,002421:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024178,002422:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024179,002423:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024180,002424:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024181,002425:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024182,002426:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024183,002427:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024184,002428:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024185,002429:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024186,002430:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024187,002431:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024188,002432:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024189,002433:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024190,002434:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024191,002435:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024192,002436:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024193,002437:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024194,002438:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024195,002439:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024196,002440:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024197,002441:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024198,002442:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024199,002443:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024200,002444:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024201,002445:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024202,002446:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024203,002447:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024204,002448:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024205,002449:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024206,002450:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024207,002451: 
024208,002452:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024209,002453:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024210,002454: 
024211,002455:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024212,002456:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024213,002457:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024214,002458: 
024215,002459:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024216,002460:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

024499,002743:                                                                                                  #  RADAR RUPT READER (R20)
024500,002744: 
024501,002745:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE
024502,002746:                                                                                                  #  DSKY LIGHTS.
024503,002747: 
024504,002748: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   RADARUPT                              
024505,002749: 25,2000                                           BANK

024507,002751: 25,3157                                           COUNT*   $$/RRUPT

024509,002753: 25,3157  E7,1453                                  EBANK=   TTOGO                                 
024510,002754: 
024511,002755: 25,3157           00006        RADAREAD           EXTEND                                         #  CONTINUATION OF INTERRUPT LEAD-IN.
024512,002756: 25,3160           04007                           ROR      SUPERBNK                              #  SUPERBNK MUST BE SAVED BECAUSE RUPT
024513,002757: 25,3161           54016                           TS       BANKRUPT                              #  MAY EXIT VIA TASKOVER.
024514,002758: 25,3162           00006                           EXTEND                                         
024515,002759: 25,3163           22012                           QXCH     QRUPT                                 
024516,002760: 
024517,002761: 
024518,002762: 25,3164           34757                           CA       SEVEN                                 #  READ AND STORE RADAR SELECT BITS
024519,002763: 25,3165           00006                           EXTEND

024521,002765: 25,3167           55332                           TS       RADBITS                               
024522,002766: 
024523,002767: 25,3170           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  IF RADAR SELECT BITS ARE ZERO, ALARM
024524,002768: 25,3171           13177                           BZF      BADRUPT                               #  WITHOUT READING DATA
024525,002769: 
024526,002770: 25,3172           30046                           CA       RNRAD                                 #  STORE RAW DATA FOR DOWNLINK.
024527,002771: 25,3173           51332                           INDEX    RADBITS

024529,002773:

024531,002775: 25,3176           13203                           TCF      WHICHRAD                              
024532,002776:

025138,003382:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025139,003383:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025140,003384: 
025141,003385: 
025142,003386:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025143,003387: 
025144,003388:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025145,003389:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025146,003390:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025147,003391: 
025148,003392:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025149,003393: 
025150,003394: 
025151,003395:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025152,003396: 
025153,003397: 
025154,003398:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025155,003399: 
025156,003400:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025157,003401:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025158,003402:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025159,003403:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025160,003404:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025161,003405: 
025162,003406: 
025163,003407:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025164,003408: 
025165,003409:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025166,003410:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025167,003411: 
025168,003412: 
025169,003413:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025170,003414:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025171,003415: 
025172,003416: 
025173,003417:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025174,003418:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025175,003419: 
025176,003420:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025177,003421: 
025178,003422:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025179,003423:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025180,003424:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025181,003425:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025182,003426:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025183,003427: 
025184,003428: 
025185,003429:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025186,003430: 
025187,003431:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 582 

025189,003433:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025190,003434:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025191,003435: 
025192,003436:                                                                                                  #     THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX,CDUY,CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
025193,003437: 
025194,003438:

025386,003630:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025387,003631:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025388,003632:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025389,003633: 
025390,003634:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025391,003635: 
025392,003636:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025393,003637:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025394,003638:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025395,003639: 
025396,003640:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025397,003641:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025398,003642:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025399,003643:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025400,003644:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025401,003645:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025402,003646:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025403,003647: 
025404,003648: 
025405,003649:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025406,003650:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025407,003651:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025408,003652: 
025409,003653:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025410,003654:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025411,003655:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025412,003656:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025413,003657:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025414,003658:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025415,003659: 
025416,003660: 
025417,003661:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025418,003662:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025419,003663:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025420,003664:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025421,003665:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025422,003666:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025423,003667:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025424,003668:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025425,003669:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025426,003670:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025427,003671:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025428,003672:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025429,003673:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025430,003674:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025431,003675:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025432,003676: 
025433,003677:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025434,003678:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
025435,003679:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

025827,004071:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025828,004072: 
025829,004073:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025830,004074:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025831,004075:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025832,004076: 
025833,004077:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025834,004078:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
025835,004079:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
025836,004080: 
025837,004081:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025838,004082:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025839,004083:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025840,004084:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025841,004085:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025842,004086:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025843,004087:

Page 596 

025845,004089:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025846,004090:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025847,004091:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025848,004092:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025849,004093:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025850,004094:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025851,004095:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025852,004096: 
025853,004097: 
025854,004098: 26,3202           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
025855,004099: 26,3203           27410                                    INTSTALL

026050,004294:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026051,004295:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026052,004296: 
026053,004297: 
026054,004298:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026055,004299: 
026056,004300:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026057,004301:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026058,004302:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026059,004303:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026060,004304: 
026061,004305: 
026062,004306:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026063,004307: 
026064,004308: 
026065,004309:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026066,004310: 
026067,004311:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026068,004312:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026069,004313:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026070,004314:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026071,004315:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026072,004316: 
026073,004317: 
026074,004318:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026075,004319: 
026076,004320: 
026077,004321:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026078,004322: 
026079,004323:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026080,004324:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026081,004325:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026082,004326: 
026083,004327:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026084,004328:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026085,004329:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026086,004330:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026087,004331: 
026088,004332:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026089,004333:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026090,004334:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026091,004335:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026092,004336:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026093,004337:
